  19 #include <stdint.h>
  20 
  21 #include "jisx0213.h"
  22 
  23 /* JISX0213 plane 1 (= ISO-IR-233) characters are in the range
  24    0x{21..7E}{21..7E}.
  25    JISX0213 plane 2 (= ISO-IR-229) characters are in the range
  26    0x{21,23..25,28,2C..2F,6E..7E}{21..7E}.
  27    Together this makes 120 rows of 94 characters.
  28 */
  29 
  30 /* Tables JISX0213 -> UCS-4.  Generated through
  31 
  32    clisp tab.lisp < JISX0213.TXT
  33 
  34    where tab.lisp is:
  35    ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
  36    (locally (declare (compile))
  37      (flet ((row-convert (row)
  38               (cond ((<= #x121 row #x17E) (- row 289)) ; 0..93
  39                     ((= #x221 row)        (- row 451)) ; 94
  40                     ((<= #x223 row #x225) (- row 452)) ; 95..97
  41                     ((= #x228 row)        (- row 454)) ; 98
  42                     ((<= #x22C row #x22F) (- row 457)) ; 99..102
  43                     ((<= #x26E row #x27E) (- row 519))))) ; 103..119
  44        (let ((table (make-array '(120 94) :initial-element 0))
  45              (pagemin (make-array #x1100 :initial-element nil))
  46              (pagemax (make-array #x1100 :initial-element nil))
  47              (pageidx (make-array #x1100 :initial-element nil))
  48              (pagestart (make-array 0 :fill-pointer 0 :adjustable t)))
  49          (let ((private-use #x0001))
  50            (loop
  51              (let ((line (read-line nil nil nil)))
  52                (unless line (return))
  53                (let ((row (parse-integer line :start 2 :end 5 :radix 16))
  54                      (col (parse-integer line :start 5 :end 7 :radix 16))
  55                      ucs)
  56                  (if (= (length line) 21)
  57                    (let ((u1 (parse-integer line :start 10 :end 14 :radix 16))
  58                          (u2 (parse-integer line :start 17 :end 21 :radix 16)))
  59                      (format t "  ~({ 0x~4,'0X, 0x~4,'0X }~),~%" u1 u2)
  60                      (setf ucs private-use)
  61                      (incf private-use))
  62                    (setf ucs (parse-integer line :start 10 :radix 16)))
  63                  (setf (aref table (row-convert row) (- col #x21)) ucs)))))
  64          (format t "~%")
  65          (dotimes (rowc 120)
  66            (dotimes (colc 94)
  67              (let* ((value (aref table rowc colc))
  68                     (page (ash value -8))
  69                     (rest (ldb (byte 8 0) value)))
  70                (setf (aref pagemin page)
  71                      (if (aref pagemin page)
  72                        (min (aref pagemin page) rest)
  73                        rest))
  74                (setf (aref pagemax page)
  75                      (if (aref pagemax page)
  76                        (max (aref pagemax page) rest)
  77                        rest)))))
  78          (let ((index 0))
  79            (do ((i 0)) ((>= i #x1100))
  80              (if (aref pagemin i)
  81                (if (and (aref pagemin (1+ i))
  82                         (>= (aref pagemin i) #x80)
  83                         (< (aref pagemax (1+ i)) #x80))
  84                  ; Combine two pages into a single one.
  85                  (progn
  86                    (vector-push-extend (+ (ash i 8) #x80) pagestart)
  87                    (setf (aref pageidx i) index)
  88                    (setf (aref pageidx (1+ i)) index)
  89                    (incf index)
  90                    (incf i 2))
  91                  ; A single page.
  92                  (progn
  93                    (vector-push-extend (ash i 8) pagestart)
  94                    (setf (aref pageidx i) index)
  95                    (incf index)
  96                    (incf i)))
  97                (incf i))))
  98          (dotimes (row #x300)
  99            (let ((rowc (row-convert row)))
 100              (when rowc
 101                (format t "  /\* 0x~X21..0x~X7E *\/~%" row row)
 102                (let ((count 0))
 103                  (dotimes (colc 94)
 104                    (when (= (mod count 8) 0) (format t " "))
 105                    (let* ((value (aref table rowc colc))
 106                           (page (ash value -8))
 107                           (index (aref pageidx page)))
 108                      (assert (<= 0 (- value (aref pagestart index)) #xFF))
 109                      (format t " ~(0x~4,'0X~),"
 110                              (logior (ash index 8)
 111                                      (- value (aref pagestart index)))))
 112                    (incf count)
 113                    (when (= (mod count 8) 0) (format t "~%"))))
 114                (format t "~%"))))
 115          (format t "~%")
 116          (let ((count 0))
 117            (dotimes (i (length pagestart))
 118              (when (= (mod count 8) 0) (format t " "))
 119              (format t " ~7<~(0x~4,'0X~)~>," (aref pagestart i))
 120              (incf count)
 121              (when (= (mod count 8) 0) (format t "~%"))))
 122          (format t "~%"))))
 123    ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
 124 */
 125

1755 /* Tables UCS-4 -> JISX0213.  Generated through
1756 
1757    clisp tab.lisp < JISX0213.TXT
1758 
1759    where tab.lisp is:
1760    ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
1761    (locally (declare (compile))
1762      (let ((table (make-array #x110000 :initial-element nil))
1763            (pages (make-array #x4400 :initial-element nil))
1764            (maxpage -1)
1765            (combining-prefixes '()))
1766        (flet ((add-entry (ucs plane row col)
1767                 (assert (<= 0 plane 1))
1768                 (assert (<= 0 row #x7f))
1769                 (assert (<= 0 col #x7f))
1770                 (setf (aref table ucs)
1771                       (logior (ash plane 15) (ash row 8) col))
1772                 (setf (aref pages (ash ucs -6)) t)
1773                 (setf maxpage (max maxpage (ash ucs -6)))))
1774          (loop
1775            (let ((line (read-line nil nil nil)))
1776              (unless line (return))
1777              (let ((plane (1- (parse-integer line :start 2 :end 3 :radix 16)))
1778                    (row (parse-integer line :start 3 :end 5 :radix 16))
1779                    (col (parse-integer line :start 5 :end 7 :radix 16)))
1780                (if (= (length line) 21)
1781                  (let ((u1 (parse-integer line :start 10 :end 14 :radix 16))
1782                        (u2 (parse-integer line :start 17 :end 21 :radix 16)))
1783                    (assert (member u2 '(#x02E5 #x02E9 #x0300 #x0301 #x309A)))
1784                    (push u1 combining-prefixes))
1785                  (let ((ucs (parse-integer line :start 10 :radix 16)))
1786                    (add-entry ucs plane row col)))))))
1787        (dolist (u1 combining-prefixes)
1788          (assert (aref table u1))
1789          (setf (aref table u1) (logior (aref table u1) #x80)))
1790        (let ((index 0))
1791          (dotimes (i (1+ maxpage))
1792            (when (= (mod i 8) 0) (format t " "))
1793            (if (aref pages i)
1794              (progn
1795                (format t " ~3D," index)
1796                (incf index))
1797              (format t " ~3D," -1))
1798            (when (= (mod (1+ i) 8) 0) (format t "~%"))))
1799        (format t "~%")
1800        (dotimes (i (1+ maxpage))
1801          (when (aref pages i)
1802            (format t "  /\* 0x~4,'0X *\/~%" (ash i 6))
1803            (do ((j 0)) ((>= j #x40))
1804              (let* ((ucs (+ (ash i 6) j))
1805                     (value (or (aref table ucs) 0)))
1806                (when (= (mod j 8) 0) (format t " "))
1807                (format t " ~(0x~4,'0X~)," value)
1808                (incf j)
1809                (when (= (mod j 8) 0) (format t "~%"))))))))
1810    ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
